  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_af76d9f6-7af2-4c2d-aa52-d7272b04f4ff'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer8119778292251710659"><b>*****FIVE BEAUTIFULLY PERFECT STARS*****</b><br/><br/><br/><b>I kissed him for making me laugh, for making me scream. I kissed him for being the only person who truly understood me, for being so impossibly like me in some ways it was a wonder we ever agreed on anything. I kissed him for being Bennett Ryan, my Beautiful Bastard.</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/588d82f4ba917d9a9e0e8f4d015a12fd_zpscvzrlyvy.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429554317i/14604697._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 588d82f4ba917d9a9e0e8f4d015a12fd_zpscvzrlyvy.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>This novella was <b>PERFECT</b> to me!! I loved everything about this one. I've decided that I'm going back and re-reading <b>"Beautiful Bastard"</b>. I've forgotten how much intense and smoking hot chem</span>
  <span id="freeText8119778292251710659" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE BEAUTIFULLY PERFECT STARS*****</b><br><br><br><b>I kissed him for making me laugh, for making me scream. I kissed him for being the only person who truly understood me, for being so impossibly like me in some ways it was a wonder we ever agreed on anything. I kissed him for being Bennett Ryan, my Beautiful Bastard.</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/588d82f4ba917d9a9e0e8f4d015a12fd_zpscvzrlyvy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429554317i/14604697._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 588d82f4ba917d9a9e0e8f4d015a12fd_zpscvzrlyvy.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This novella was <b>PERFECT</b> to me!! I loved everything about this one. I've decided that I'm going back and re-reading <b>"Beautiful Bastard"</b>. I've forgotten how much intense and smoking hot chemistry that Bennett and Chloe had. I was wishing the entire time that I could jump into this story and take Chloe's place!!<br><br><br><br><br>A week before their wedding in San Diego, Bennett decides that the two should abstain from sex in order to make their first night as husband &amp; wife, even more amazing. Chloe is definitely not on board with this plan, and she will pull out all the stops to get Bennett to change his mind. After two years of being together, their sex life is better than ever. These two bring major steam!! They are so into each other that sometimes they forget that they're out in public with family and friends!! I freaking <b>LOVE</b> their passion!!!<br><br><br><br><br>We get just the perfect dose of their friends and crazy family too. I loved getting more time with Will, Max, and even George!! Bennett and Chloe not only have to deal with unbearable sexual tension, but numerous things that can potentially ruin their wedding day. I can't imagine the story going any other way for this couple. It was a perfect story and a <b>PERFECT HEA</b> for me!! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2566632893213467249"><b>FANFUCKINGTASTIC.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043464.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's finally arrived. All the hate fucking, all the arguments and torn panties... it's all led to this moment. The moment where Chloe & Bennett <b>tie the fucking knot</b>.<br/><br/>Gah! This series just needs to go on forever and I'd be on cloud nine. But nope, we have to say goodbye to these six crazy kids. In true BB fashion, Chloe and Bennett are completely insane. We get to see a softer side during moments in this where Chloe and Bennett are both hit with just how much they love each other,</span>
  <span id="freeText2566632893213467249" style="display:none"><b>FANFUCKINGTASTIC.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043464.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's finally arrived. All the hate fucking, all the arguments and torn panties... it's all led to this moment. The moment where Chloe &amp; Bennett <b>tie the fucking knot</b>.<br><br>Gah! This series just needs to go on forever and I'd be on cloud nine. But nope, we have to say goodbye to these six crazy kids. In true BB fashion, Chloe and Bennett are completely insane. We get to see a softer side during moments in this where Chloe and Bennett are both hit with just how much they love each other, but in the end it is the hate in this love/hate relationship that had me making unladylike snorting noises throughout this final installment.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043465.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although we do get the whole gang, part of me wanted just a tad bit more of Will &amp; Hanna. But we get to see a great glimpse into how their lives will play out. Each time I get a bit more Bennett it makes me doubt just which man I love more. Each one holds a special place in my heart for different reasons. For Bennett, it's the need to argue, tear expensive panties and to take Chloe whenever the need hits him. For Max, it's the accent, throwing around words like <i>smashing</i> and his urges for fucking just about anywhere he might get caught. And oh, Will, him standing his ground about not falling in love and then falling hard, his smart mouth and just how quick he was going to lay claim to the girl that stole his heart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043466._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Who would have imagined these two would survive the courtship and actually make it down the aisle? Christina &amp; Lauren created such wonderful characters with such quick wit and so many memorable moments. I know that we are going to get plenty more from these two, but part of me will always hold this series close to my heart. Maybe if we all beg we might see a novella down the road to give us all just one last taste.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043467.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385005719i/7043468._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

Also really enjoyed having all the other couples in the book. <br><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/user/jbrandoncooper/media/6f063b14-e1d2-436b-80b1-03750cbf1bc9_zpschwzi8jf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>-"I think you're the best thing that's ever happened to me."<br><br>-I'd been my best and worst self with this man, and he only loved me more the more real I was with him. No place was safer for me than with Bennett.<br><br>-I was his and he was mine.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13233784782089546343" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_665773499" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/665773499" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/665773499?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lol-moments">i-lol-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-humor">genre-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-ipad">z-own-for-ipad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-billionaires-and-executives">c-billionaires-and-executives</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-completed">series-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=favorite-romantic-series">favorite-romantic-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665773499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16797083242318320099"><b>The end of the Beautiful Bastard series is the crown jewel of series conclusions. All the Strangers & Players gather together to watch Bennett & Chloe tie the knot!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386763807ra/7438318.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I think it's perfectly natural to be uneasy about starting the final book in a series. We're apprehensive about the end, and wanting the best for all the characters we've grown to love... And this is a <i>wedding</i> conclusion, so the threat of an overly sweet happily ever after was looming. However, the authors stayed true to the previous </b></span>
  <span id="freeText16797083242318320099" style="display:none"><b>The end of the Beautiful Bastard series is the crown jewel of series conclusions. All the Strangers &amp; Players gather together to watch Bennett &amp; Chloe tie the knot!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386763807ra/7438318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I think it's perfectly natural to be uneasy about starting the final book in a series. We're apprehensive about the end, and wanting the best for all the characters we've grown to love... And this is a <i>wedding</i> conclusion, so the threat of an overly sweet happily ever after was looming. However, the authors stayed true to the previous books in the series, so we laughed, swooned, squirmed, face-palmed, and cried a few happy tears...</b><br><br>This book sees the entire group (plus 300ish friends and family) gathered in sunny California for the highly anticipated beach wedding of <s>Bastard &amp; Shrew</s> Bennett Ryan &amp; Chloe Mills...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388085988ra/7734920.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We have all of the requisite family drama complete with stressed mothers, clueless fathers, tacky uncles, crass cousins, and cougar aunts... Oh by the way, am I the only one who got a Patty &amp; Selma vibe from Chloe's Aunts??<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387899507ra/7694857.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The BIG amusement in the first few pages of this book, is that Bennett decides that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he &amp; Chloe need to be chaste until their wedding night... That's right... No Sex for the couple who couldn't even manage to keep their hands off each other when it threatened to tank their careers... If at all possible, the <i>Sexbargo</i> (as Will so eloquently calls it) between Bennett &amp; Chloe managed to increase the sexual tension between the couple to levels unseen since the first half of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bastard</a>. <b><i>Which was awesome...</i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387899507ra/7694858.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So while the main couple is grappling with the poor decision making skills of the Groom, the stress of trying to pull off the Wedding of the Century is wearing on everyone. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Some sort of Wedding Murphy's Law is ruling the entire week, and everything that <i>can</i> go wrong, <i>does</i> go wrong... Watching everyone scramble to attempt to salvage this wedding was infinitely entertaining! <br><br>In the end, Bennett &amp; Chloe manage to have a memorable wedding, filled with all the overwhelming love that got them this far. <blockquote><b><i>I was getting married tomorrow.<br>To Bennett Ryan.<br>To the man who’d anger-fucked me into loving him.</i></b></blockquote> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388068986ra/7732509.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote><b><i>“Holy shit. You’re my </i>wife<i>.”<br>Laughing, I said, “We’re married. That’s <i>insane</i>. Who let this happen?”<br>He didn't even break a smile. Instead, his eyes grew heavy, his voice even lower. “I’m going to disrespect the </i>fuck<i> out of you later.”</i></b></blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>So we know what happened with the Beautiful Bastard &amp; his Harpy Shrew... How is life treating our other two Beautiful Couples?<br><br>Max &amp; Sara:</b><br>We learned in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17831614.Beautiful_Player__Beautiful_Bastard___3_" title="Beautiful Player (Beautiful Bastard, #3) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Player</a> that Max &amp; Sara are <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[expecting a baby... She's blissfully pregnant and max is still head over heels for her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Will &amp; Hanna:</b><br>After being stalked by Chloe's Cougar Aunts all week, Will <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[picks up a microphone and proposes to Hanna at the Rehearsal Dinner... She says yes... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>And so, we finally get our sweet Happy Ending for the Whole Gang...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382151865ra/5701756.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Since this is the Final Book (sigh) in the Beautiful Bastard Series, I would like to go ahead and present my reasons for including these books on my "Favorite Romantic Series" Shelf… Which (in my humble opinion) is a place of honor…</b><br><br>1. I love that each book had a dual Point of View between the main characters, so we had the opportunity to see things from both perspectives.<br>2. I love that the men fell just as hard as the women… Sometimes harder…<br>3. The witty banter between characters had me cracking from the first lines of Beautiful bastard to the last line of beautiful beginning...<br>4. All of the women were smart and strong. Nobody was an idiot, even if they suffered the occasional idiotic moment. <br>5. These characters are all fairly believable… Nobody is untouchable (emotionally, financially, or otherwise) I get the feeling that I could stumble across these six people grabbing drinks and pub food in Manhattan... And I'd kind of like to sit in on one of their hilarious conversations. <br>6. All of the angst was reserved for self-exploration, and for coming to grips with the overwhelming feeling of falling in love.<br>7. I loved that each character returned in full force for each subsequent book until we had a well rounded group of six individuals I was invested in. <br>8. I suppose I need to mention that this series has a variety of wild sexy-times, the most jaw dropping dirty talk, and some seriously scrumptious boyfriends. <br>9. There was a voice and a rhythm to these books that I'd never experienced before... Blending humor, sweet honest emotion, and raw passionate sex.<br><br><b>This whole series is primed for a re-read in my future... They are that much fun. I can definitely see myself coming back to this series in a few years and still having a ball.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387899613ra/7694878.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Some of My Favorite Moments from Beautiful Beginning:</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I needed a minute to relish the effects of the Mighty Bennett Ryan Oralgasm.<br>“That was so fucking <i>good</i>,” I mumbled, catching my breath. “I think your mouth is its own Greek god. Tongueseus.”<br><br><b>Bennett thinking about Cousin <i>Bull</i>:</b><br>I made a mental note to call a friend of mine at the IRS and have him audited.<br>I was only kidding. Mostly.<br><br><b>Bennett thinking about Will:</b><br>I missed his insistence that we were a bunch of pussies. God, he was the biggest fucking pussy now.<br><br>Bennett Ryan was a swoony fucking bastard, and tonight—stupid chastity rule or not—I was going to ride him like a horse.<br><br>Even in the dim light I could see the rage and lust on his face. My favorite fucking Bennett.<br><br>“We’re talking about Plan Chastity,” Max explained.<br>“Oh, good,” Will said, turning to face me. “If I may, this sexbargo thing may be the dumbest thing I’ve ever heard.”<br><br>He was apologizing for being an ass. My apology was letting him do it.<br><br>“The psychotic clown I sent for his birthday will feel like a feather falling on a pillow atop a cloud. The laxative in my lunch? Child’s play. If you think it was bad when I sent that fake resumé for his open assistant position and the stripper came for the interview? No. We’re talking Defcon Five, <i>Vietcong</i>-level mind fucking, do you hear me, Chloe?”<br>“Can’t wait, Dr. Sumner.”<br>He pulled back, studying me. “It’s a little unnerving how <i>excited</i> you look.”<br>Straightening up, I pushed off the wall and patted his cheek. “I <i>am</i> excited. I like seeing that the only thing that will change after this week is that Bennett will have a ring on his finger and my last name after his first name. I like knowing that you guys will continue to escalate this big testicle war. You and Hanna will continue to be adorable and giddy, Max and Sara will continue to be disgustingly in love. Bennett will continue to alternately rock my world and make me insane. It’s life as it should be.”<br><br>“I’m not feeling particularly gentle tonight.”<br>Arching my neck, I gave his mouth better access to the most vulnerable part of my throat, whispering, “Good. I don’t want you slow and sweet.”<br>“But it’s our <i>wedding</i> night,” he argued with mock sincerity. “Shouldn't I gently lay you on a feather bed and bring you endless, loving pleasure?”<br>I reached for his hand, pressed it harder into me. “You can do that when I’m bruised and sore afterwards, in the middle of the night.”<br><br>“I fucking <i>love</i> your mouth.” He leaned forward, laughing against my lips. “And I love fucking your mouth.”<br><br>“What kind of monster are you?” I teased, lightly scratching his stomach.<br>His answering smile tilted up one half of his perfect mouth. “The kind that’s going to fuck you so hard it’ll look like your legs were put on backwards.”<br><br>“We’re married,” he said quietly, pressing another kiss to my belly button. “I’m your safe place. I've always been your safe place.”<br><br>...we would forever be the fevered combination of Bennett and Chloe. Mr. Ryan and Miss Mills. Mr. Mills and Mrs. Ryan. Husband and wife. Bastard and bitch.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><b>

<div id="review_796877570" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/796877570" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/796877570?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Christina Lauren Fans, Romance</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Wendy'sThoughts by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer796877570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6294895614488623293"><b>4.5 Anticipating, Feverish, Hopeful, Antagonistic Ever After Stars<br/> * * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>This was the last book of an amazing series. This was the ramp up to the wedding of Bennett and Chloe, who we met in the first book, Beautiful Bastard. Now if you have been following my journey with these characters, you will have seen the progression the series has taken. <br/><br/>When I first met this couple… I had to put myself into an understanding of this fantasy land of where they worked and lived… and once I</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6294895614488623293" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Anticipating, Feverish, Hopeful, Antagonistic Ever After Stars<br> * * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>This was the last book of an amazing series. This was the ramp up to the wedding of Bennett and Chloe, who we met in the first book, Beautiful Bastard. Now if you have been following my journey with these characters, you will have seen the progression the series has taken. <br><br>When I first met this couple… I had to put myself into an understanding of this fantasy land of where they worked and lived… and once I did that… I was good to go. I lived through their unconventional courtship dance and took the rest of their friends’ journeys through the following books of the series. <br><br>The experiences leading up to this finale has been nothing but AWESOME. The humor mixed with real concerns showed the growth of the all of the characters as well as the authors. </b><br><br>For what started out in my head as a little time spent with some smutty fun, turned out to be...<br><br>Days of bliss… <br>Days of wanting to be part of this click… <br>Days of thinking about what people like them in our world are doing right now and how I hope they are having as much fun as the ones in these books are… <br><br>Because “they” say… you should write what you know… that by taking something you are familiar with will make the story easier and more real… then these authors know some really fantastic things. <br><br>They have experienced or have figured out great dialogue and comic timing… they have had amazing sex with real emotions attached… or just figured out how to write it… and best of all, they have met people they love and want to share… because every single character written, for me, felt authentic and someone I either really wanted to know… or have had the experience of meeting somewhere…<br><br>So, this review isn’t so much about this particular book… because let’s admit it … if you are reading this you probably are someone who has been reading the series and checking out the last part.<br>What I will say about this part is that it was a perfect ending with everything you came to expect about this couple… I even had tears during the wedding. <br><br>Lastly…. I would like to share one of the main reasons this series was so much fun, Shurrn. We did a Buddy Read that was hysterical. We ended up texting each other continuously and what was said back and forth during these reads was priceless. To have such an instant connection and be constantly giggling and laughing beyond the norm… it is something I wish for all of you to experience.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_2772458733" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2772458733" />
    <a title="Brooke — brooklynnnnereads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47221787-brooke-brooklynnnnereads"><img alt="Brooke — brooklynnnnereads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600143980p2/47221787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2772458733?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brooke — brooklynnnnereads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brooke — brooklynnnnereads" href="/user/show/47221787-brooke-brooklynnnnereads">Brooke — brooklynnnnereads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476755106" href="/book/show/18051336-beautiful-beginning">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2772458733" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12414389416714163767">Yes, yes, yes! I liked this novella so much more than I expected I would and I'm so happy about it!<br/><br/>Initially, I was apprehensive to pick up any of the novellas in this series because I felt that I got enough from the story in the main novel related to the couple involved. However, I loved this novella and it really packed a punch in such a short page count. <br/><br/>First, I LOVED the plot line of "waiting" until the wedding, even if I can see how people could make it into something being problematic. Ma</span>
  <span id="freeText12414389416714163767" style="display:none">Yes, yes, yes! I liked this novella so much more than I expected I would and I'm so happy about it!<br /><br />Initially, I was apprehensive to pick up any of the novellas in this series because I felt that I got enough from the story in the main novel related to the couple involved. However, I loved this novella and it really packed a punch in such a short page count. <br /><br />First, I LOVED the plot line of "waiting" until the wedding, even if I can see how people could make it into something being problematic. Maybe it's just me but man, that tension.....I'm all about it. <br /><br />Also, I feel like I may have liked the couple more in this novella than I actually did in the main novel "Beautiful Bastard". It has been awhile since I read that initial novel in the series so I could be wrong, but I really liked the couple and their chemistry in this book but don't remember liking them as much before. <br /><br />This novella was so good that I could have easily read more. I could have read a full length novel related to this wedding and this couple and I would have been sold! Not only will I definitely be reading more written by Christina Lauren but I will be checking out more of the novellas in this series. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="╰☆╮ LovesToRead ╰☆╮" class="user" itemprop="url" name="╰☆╮ LovesToRead ╰☆╮" href="/user/show/5725009-lovestoread">╰☆╮ LovesToRead ╰☆╮</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646329681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4478293291488274957">to know this is where the story ends is an offense perpetrated upon the readers and the characters within the pages by the authors we expect to do right by both.<br/><br/>the moment this series veered off course and put the focus on a new man, whether a "Player" or a "Stranger," the authors forced the readers to become invested not just in that male, but the welfare of his heart and happiness....not to mention a new couple.<br/><br/>this book follows the journey to the altar for Bennett and Chloe, but ends on the n</span>
  <span id="freeText4478293291488274957" style="display:none">to know this is where the story ends is an offense perpetrated upon the readers and the characters within the pages by the authors we expect to do right by both.<br /><br />the moment this series veered off course and put the focus on a new man, whether a "Player" or a "Stranger," the authors forced the readers to become invested not just in that male, but the welfare of his heart and happiness....not to mention a new couple.<br /><br />this book follows the journey to the altar for Bennett and Chloe, but ends on the night of their wedding....<br /><br />no honeymoon<br /><br />No baby for Max and Sara...or maybe their wedding<br /><br />and how about Will and Hannah? he proposed at the rehearsal dinner, yet we seem to be destined to be denied the pleasure of those events and the knowledge of the happiness in characters we, as readers, have become invested in.<br /><br />I'm both shocked and offended by how this ended and, as a result, it literally took away from this book for me. to deny us a true happily ever after for the remaining characters is just heinous...<br /><br />I feel shafted...to know that we as readers became invested in two other couples...fell for a "Stranger" and a "Player"...only to be left wondering about the other two couples and the lives they appear to have ahead of them...babies...weddings of their own. <br /><br />It's absolutely shameful that the authors had no issue taking our money by dangling the proverbial carrots in front of us in the form of Will and Max only to never truly allow us to taste them completely by giving us their entire story.<br /><br />Add that to the fact that Chloe got on my last nerve with her narcissistic, selfish b*tchy behavior and this was a very disappointing INSTALLMENT for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4478293291488274957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/664120279?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476751740" href="/book/show/17839081-beautiful-beginning">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664120279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14937227473734150289"><b>Beautiful Beginning is a Beautiful ending to this awesome series!!! I loved it.</b> <br/><br/>Ahhhhh I know I say it every time but this has got to be the funniest, sweetest, sexiest of all the beautiful books. <br/><br/><b>Christina and Lauren are pure fucking comic genuises....AND I MEAN THAT! I was rolling. I was holding my stomach. I was snorting. I was dying laughing. It wasn't pretty but there was no help for it!</b><br/><br/><br/>This story is one that we've all been waiting for. The story of both BBs getting married!!! That in it se</span>
  <span id="freeText14937227473734150289" style="display:none"><b>Beautiful Beginning is a Beautiful ending to this awesome series!!! I loved it.</b> <br><br>Ahhhhh I know I say it every time but this has got to be the funniest, sweetest, sexiest of all the beautiful books. <br><br><b>Christina and Lauren are pure fucking comic genuises....AND I MEAN THAT! I was rolling. I was holding my stomach. I was snorting. I was dying laughing. It wasn't pretty but there was no help for it!</b><br><br><br>This story is one that we've all been waiting for. The story of both BBs getting married!!! That in it self sets up for an awesome story. Well this book <b>does not</b> disappoint. I loved it from the first line to the last. Christina and Lauren masterfully spins the tales and portrays the scenes to perfection. But not only do they do those perfectly but they have an amazing way of making me feel and understand the love (and pretend hate) that these two have. Even the other characters are rich! Yes - rich is an awesome word for how they weave their spell on me. I'm in for the ride from start to finish. <br><br>I cannot gush enough about how much I loved these Beautiful books and I'm really going to miss all these characters but I will be visiting them again! <br> <br>Ok so this gets 5 stars because it's perfectly written. It's not just funny. Funny is too tame a word. It's fucking hilarious!!! The kind that you are laughing so hard and so often that you do start to question your sanity. Then you have the colorful characters and their perfect chemistry with each other. Each character is perfectly different, perfectly portrayed, perfectly awesome. You of course have the hot sexy scenes that Christina Lauren has perfected. You have the chemistry and of course the LOVE that you feel with all three couples but especially beautifully written between Chloe and Bennett. Their love (especially Bennett's) leaps off the pages and into your heart!!!! <br><br>Ok so did I use the word perfect enough times or what???? I guess to sum it up... LOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOVED IT!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402500477i/9946264.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1425298898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18387652362182450203"><b>4.5 hot and hilarous stars </b><br/><br/>OMG, this novella is SO much fun! The gang all gather together for Bennett and Chloe's wedding with all kinds of pranks, madness, the odd disaster or two and sexy shenanigans galore - and quite possibly the funniest wedding rehearsal EVER (dry humping at the altar, LMAO!)!<br/><br/>Bennett and Chloe are at their explosive best, their families are a riot, Max and Will are both in fine form, and with Bennett's insistance on remaining 'chaste' until the wedding night, the smutty te</span>
  <span id="freeText18387652362182450203" style="display:none"><b>4.5 hot and hilarous stars </b><br /><br />OMG, this novella is SO much fun! The gang all gather together for Bennett and Chloe's wedding with all kinds of pranks, madness, the odd disaster or two and sexy shenanigans galore - and quite possibly the funniest wedding rehearsal EVER (dry humping at the altar, LMAO!)!<br /><br />Bennett and Chloe are at their explosive best, their families are a riot, Max and Will are both in fine form, and with Bennett's insistance on remaining 'chaste' until the wedding night, the smutty teasing is hilarious!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Tonight,” he growled, returning to my neck. “Tonight I’m going to consummate this marriage so fucking hard you’re going to walk with a limp on that beach in Fiji.” <br /><br />“Bennett Ryan was a swoony fucking bastard, and tonight—stupid chastity rule or not—I was going to ride him like a horse.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Written in dual POV, and with the audiobook narrated by Grace Grant and Sebastian York (who has quite possibly the sexiest voice on audio), I loved every moment of this quick read.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“We're married. I'm your safe place. I've always been your safe place.” </i>
</blockquote><br />Laugh-out-loud funny, sexy and beautifully romantic, if you're a fan of this series, this one cannot be missed.<br /><br />4.5 stars.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3991905102930953262">I listened to the Audible version of this book and I have to say that it was fantastic! It's been quite a while since I've read Bennett and Chloe's story in 'Beautiful Bastard'. I have to admit that I was a little hazy on the details at first. However, it came back to me in no time.<br/><br/>It turns out that this was the series finale, which I didn't realize. I meant to read them in order, but goofed up. In the end, I'm not sure that it really made a difference. I don't feel like I missed anything and I </span>
  <span id="freeText3991905102930953262" style="display:none">I listened to the Audible version of this book and I have to say that it was fantastic! It's been quite a while since I've read Bennett and Chloe's story in 'Beautiful Bastard'. I have to admit that I was a little hazy on the details at first. However, it came back to me in no time.<br /><br />It turns out that this was the series finale, which I didn't realize. I meant to read them in order, but goofed up. In the end, I'm not sure that it really made a difference. I don't feel like I missed anything and I thoroughly enjoyed the book.<br /><br />This book focuses on the wedding, and week leading up to the wedding, of Chloe and Bennett. Bennett decides that he is going to abstain from sex for the week leading up to the wedding, which resulted in a lot of sexual frustration and some comical situations. That seems to be the entire focus of the first 1/2 to 3/4 of the book. It was funny at times, but I have to admit that it did get a little old.<br /><br />All of the sexual tension comes to a head at the wedding rehearsal, when we finally get another taste of the sharp-tongued pair that we fell in love with in 'Beautiful Bastard'. I was practically rolling on the floor with laughter. Suddenly, I remembered why I loved this couple so much. The rehearsal had to be my favorite part of the book.<br /><br />There is a lot of last-minute wedding disasters, but none that stop the main event. It was predictable, but still funny. In the end, we get a HEA and this feisty couple rides off into the sunset. The only thing I would've changed was to make this book shorter. In my opinion, this book could have been done in a much shorter novella, without some of the fluff. The story was fun, but did drag at times.</span>

They felt the love and dealt with each others crazy ideas and outbursts.<br />I enjoyed every filthy comment and every funny prank. I loved how they didn't care how the wedding turned out because they were enjoying themselves and knew that what mattered was that they'll finally be together forever.<br />Nowadays people put soooo much effort into their wedding and by the end of the night they won't be as pleased as Bennet and Chloe were even thought their wedding was a disaster.<br /><br /><b> “You found the one person who not only can handle you, but wants to handle you.” </b><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_734989371" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734989371" />
    <a title="Christine (Shh Moms Reading)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5334715-christine-shh-moms-reading"><img alt="Christine (Shh Moms Reading)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406862375p2/5334715.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734989371?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine (Shh Moms Reading)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine (Shh Moms Reading)" href="/user/show/5334715-christine-shh-moms-reading">Christine (Shh Moms Reading)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734989371" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9868532610736404538">This was so much fun for me to read and such a nice break from the more serious reads I have been reading lately. Christina Lauren are new authors to me and ones I will undoubtedly read again over and over. This series is witty, sarcastic and a just plain fun series filled with funny banter, hot sex and ultimately love found. I devoured this series – one book a day not being able to put down the book until I finished the series. Christina Lauren have a great dynamic working together, it was seam</span>
  <span id="freeText9868532610736404538" style="display:none">This was so much fun for me to read and such a nice break from the more serious reads I have been reading lately. Christina Lauren are new authors to me and ones I will undoubtedly read again over and over. This series is witty, sarcastic and a just plain fun series filled with funny banter, hot sex and ultimately love found. I devoured this series – one book a day not being able to put down the book until I finished the series. Christina Lauren have a great dynamic working together, it was seamless and effortless and I look forward to seeing more from them in the future. Excuse me in advance for the lengthy review as I will be reviewing all 6 books together :) <br /><br />The series starts off with Beautiful Bastard where we meet Bennett Ryan and Chloe Mills. Chloe is Bennett’s right hand woman and assistant. Bennett has returned home from 9 months in Paris to work at his family’s business and what ensues between these two is an illicit HOT office affair complete with panty ripping and hot dirty talk. I’ll admit that it felt so wrong, I was often scared that they would be found out but I LOVED every moment I spent with them. Seeing these two, who are so alike in so many ways, interact with each other, try to fight their attraction for each other made me fall in love with them HARD as I rooted for them to work out as a couple. As a reader, I recognized that it was so much more than casual sex and in my heart, I wished that they would be able to see the same. Will they be able to face their vulnerabilities and their fears about love and be able to let each other in? Or will Bennett forever be a Beautiful Bastard?<br /><br />I enjoyed the novella Beautiful Bitch which follows the story line immediately following Beautiful Bastard. Without revealing too much of what happens and the outcome of Beautiful Bastard, this was a fast, hot and steamy read showing the different obstacles that any couple face while acknowledging the importance of moving forward and home.<br /><br />Beautiful Stranger begins where Ryan Media has now created a smaller office in NYC. We see our beloved characters from the previous books however this is the story about the secondary characters of Max Stella, a British, handsome and successful venture capitalist and friend of Bennett and Sara Dillon, friend to Chloe and Director of Finance for Ryan Media. Unfortunately Sara has suffered a lot of pain and heartache from her cheating ex and has moved to NYC to start over – new job, new home, new life, new Sara. She meets a beautiful stranger while at a club in NYC and experiences her very first ever exhibitionist orgasmic sex and now has a taste for sex in places where the possibilities of being seen/caught are high. Max and Sara’s attraction to each other is undeniable. Not only that, it is completely HOT and mouthwatering. It was completely amazing to me to watch this couple with their no strings commitment try to fight something that was obvious to me as a reader. They were playing a dangerous game where feelings are bound to grow beyond a “sexual agreement”. Has Max met his match and will Sara be able to let down her walls to let this Beautiful Stranger into her heart?<br /><br />Beautiful Bombshell was another great accompaniment to the Beautiful Bastard Series. Bennett is celebrating his bachelor party in Vegas with his boys. The lengths that the “taken” boys would go to to be with their women is hysterical. Ahhhh to be loved so much! &lt;3<br /><br />In Beautiful Player, we finally get Will Sumner’s story. Oh Will – he is my FAVE from the entire series and that is saying a lot because I really LOVED them all!! Will helps his best friend from college out by taking his younger sister, Hanna Bergstrom under his wing to help her live life and enjoy being 24. Hanna is a serious, no frills kinda girl – more interested in her grad school science studies than dating, having friends and her social life. Ziggy, as she is known to her family has always crushed on Will and I am beyond ECSTATIC for him to teach her how to be less of a nerd and how to date. I totally loved Hanna – she is so different from other MC’s in that she is a combination of silly, confident, pretty without realizing it and having ZERO filter. Will and Ziggy are playful and fun and I found myself smiling a lot throughout my read of their book. It’s hard in my opinion to try to “teach” someone how to be hot and experienced in all ways and I knew that this story would lead to unchartered territory for them both. This was the HOTTEST and SEXIEST book of the series (i.e. the sexting, the hand jobs, OMG). What I found most sexy is that Will is teaching Hanna everything he knows and in the process realizing truths about himself as a player. This relationship was combustible and earth shattering….but can a player stop his player ways and finally settle down? And will Hanna stop following the rules to let her Beautiful Player into her heart and life and live life to the fullest? <br /><br />Beautiful Beginning is the final book in this wonderful series. This novella goes back to our first couple Bennett and Chloe as they are finally on their way to the alter. I love how much this couple has grown together yet there are still so many things about them that haven’t changed – their undying love for each other, their confidence in themselves and their love and relationship and their constant need for the physical aspect between them that makes them SO DAMN HOT! I don’t want to spoil this book for anyone as it releases in a couple of days but I admire Bennett’s strength, I laughed out loud to Chloe’s antics to defy Bennett’s wishes and a bunch of scenes had me laughing out loud. This couple is always surrounded by constant chaos and yes there are people who are slightly dysfunctional but through it all – the message is quite clear – this is a family filled with a lot of love and mutual respect for one another – this is a beautiful family whose journey I enjoyed experiencing and I am definitely sad to see them go. <br /><br />I know that this is the final in the series but I do hope to one day see more of Max and Sara and Will and Hanna – though their stories are complete, to see ahead a couple of years would be a real treat :) <br /><br />Thank you to Christina Lauren to writing such a wonderful series and about such a great cast of characters – I enjoyed everything about this series and look forward to reading what you have for us next! Xoxo<br /><br /><br />Stop by <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.shhmomsreading.com">www.shhmomsreading.com</a> on 11/17 for a guest post from Christina Lauren re: music playlist from Beautiful Player </span>
  <a data-text-id="9868532610736404538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_628114355" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/628114355" />
    <a title="Wendy ⏃: ✦Cheeky Chicks Blogger✦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6135885-wendy-cheeky-chicks-blogger"><img alt="Wendy ⏃: ✦Cheeky Chicks Blogger✦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534031038p2/6135885.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/628114355?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy ⏃: ✦Cheeky Chicks Blogger✦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy ⏃: ✦Cheeky Chicks Blogger✦" href="/user/show/6135885-wendy-cheeky-chicks-blogger">Wendy ⏃: ✦Cheeky Chicks Blogger✦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476755106" href="/book/show/18051336-beautiful-beginning">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6135885-wendy-cheeky-chicks-blogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6135885-wendy-cheeky-chicks-blogger?shelf=hilarious-humor-lol">hilarious-humor-lol</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6135885-wendy-cheeky-chicks-blogger?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer628114355" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10122527206616864885"><b>"ONE BEAUTIFUL BASTARD OF A GROOM. THE MOST BEAUTIFUL BITCH OF A BRIDE. A PANTY-RIPPING OFFICE HOOK-UP TURNED TRUE LOVE EVERLASTING."</b><br/><br/>This was the perfect ending to a perfect series. I’m so sad that it has come to an end but at the same time I’m very happy because I got the opportunity to know & fall in love with these amazing characters. There wasn't a moment where I didn't laugh out loud or I fanned myself because the sex was so fucking hot & steamy. We fell in love with the bastard & the bitch</span>
  <span id="freeText10122527206616864885" style="display:none"><b>"ONE BEAUTIFUL BASTARD OF A GROOM. THE MOST BEAUTIFUL BITCH OF A BRIDE. A PANTY-RIPPING OFFICE HOOK-UP TURNED TRUE LOVE EVERLASTING."</b><br><br>This was the perfect ending to a perfect series. I’m so sad that it has come to an end but at the same time I’m very happy because I got the opportunity to know &amp; fall in love with these amazing characters. There wasn't a moment where I didn't laugh out loud or I fanned myself because the sex was so fucking hot &amp; steamy. We fell in love with the bastard &amp; the bitch; these fierce, clever, amusing, funny, enthralling couple. <br><br>I loved, loved, loved this novella! Once again we were brought back to the essence that is <b>Bennett &amp; Chloe</b>. We saw them banter &amp; be playful with one another like only they know how. It was sassy, hilarious, witty, naughty, sexy, &amp; fun! The adventure that was their wedding was epic. I loved the <b>Will, Bennett, &amp; Max show</b>. Seriously, this book wouldn't be great if it didn't have the bromance of those three sexy, gorgeous men. They had me in a fit of laughter &amp; the moments with the families, the crazy aunts, &amp; everything in between was just perfect.<br><br>OMG the wedding! I was a mess okay, because it was so beautiful &amp; I consider Bennett &amp; Chloe to be my babies &amp; to witness how far they’ve gotten &amp; see them married, made me so fucking happy. <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2w7hiq8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385005967ra/7043517.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I felt like I was a part of them. I could ramble on &amp; on about this novella but really there are simply no words. This series has become very special to me &amp; I’m humbled to be a part of it. Even when the story was about Ben &amp; Chlo, we still got Max &amp; Sara &amp; Will &amp; Hanna moments; they were small but very significant. Its bittersweet to have come full circle. Bennett &amp; Chloe couldn't have been more together for each other. Overall, this was a crazy, loving, snarky story that will have you smiling until the end. <br><br><b>Christina &amp; Lauren, thank you so much for giving me these amazing stories, &amp; these amazing characters. I bow down to you &amp; I’m still crossing my fingers for more Max &amp; Sara &amp; Will &amp; Hanna. Maybe an epilogue of ‘10 years later’ &amp; everyone has babies &amp; it’s all happiness, fun, &amp; filled with lots of love &amp; passion*sigh* (to dream lol).</b> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ms2gdu" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385005967ra/7043518.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>This is definitely a series I plan on re-reading!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I kissed him for being the only person who truly understood me, for being so impossibly like me in some ways it was a wonder we ever agreed on anything.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I...knew we would forever be the fevered combination of Bennett and Chloe. Mr. Ryan and Miss Mills. Mr. Mills and Mrs. Ryan. Husband and wife. Bastard and bitch.”</i>
</b><br></span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_18775203'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775203-rusty-nailed"><img alt="Rusty Nailed (Cocktail, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1470670923l/18775203._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4ijDiwuq8IHHWfBeziKOVGETWbgUEm4GSuX1JTg2g0Y5ID+G1DEZc6asJ44XaILB2GUDoj+fi1Q8yoANj+8wqA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
